Kubernetes v1.32.0, CNI (Container Network Interface) integration is not implemented directly in the kubelet binary — it is delegated to the container runtime (e.g., containerd, CRI-O) via the CRI (Container Runtime Interface) gRPC protocol. The kubelet communicates with the runtime using CRI, and the runtime invokes CNI plugins. The relevant source files are:\\n\\n**Network Plugin Manager (coordinates CNI calls during pod creation):**\\n- `pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/kuberuntime_manager.go`: Defines `kubeGenericRuntimeManager`, the central runtime manager. Its `SyncPod` method orchestrates pod lifecycle and calls `createPodSandbox` when a new sandbox is needed. Its `UpdatePodCIDR` method passes pod CIDR to the runtime via `UpdateRuntimeConfig`, which in turn tells the runtime what CIDR to hand to CNI for IPAM.\\n\\n**CNI Plugin Invocation (via CRI RunPodSandbox):**\\n- `pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/kuberuntime_sandbox.go`: Implements `createPodSandbox`, which calls `m.runtimeService.RunPodSandbox(...)`. When the container runtime receives this call, it invokes the configured CNI plugin to set up the pod network. Also contains `generatePodSandboxConfig` (builds the sandbox config passed to the runtime) and `determinePodSandboxIPs` (reads back the IP assigned by CNI).\\n- `pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/instrumented_services.go`: Wraps `RunPodSandbox` with metrics instrumentation (`instrumentedRuntimeService`).\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-client/pkg/remote_runtime.go`: The gRPC client that actually sends `RunPodSandboxRequest` over the wire to the container runtime's CRI endpoint.\\n\\n**Network Namespace Setup:**\\n- `pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/util/util.go`: Contains `NetworkNamespaceForPod` (determines whether a pod uses pod-level or node-level network namespace), `NamespacesForPod` (builds the full `NamespaceOption` including network namespace mode), and `PodSandboxChanged` (detects if the sandbox needs recreation, including network namespace changes).\\n- `pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/kuberuntime_sandbox.go`: `generatePodSandboxLinuxConfig` sets the `NamespaceOptions` (including network namespace) in the Linux sandbox config sent to the runtime.\\n\\n**IPAM (IP Address Management):**\\n- CNI IPAM plugin invocation happens inside the container runtime. From the Kubernetes control-plane side, node-level CIDR allocation (which feeds into CNI IPAM) is handled by:\\n  - `pkg/controller/nodeipam/node_ipam_controller.go`: The node IPAM controller (`Controller`, `NewNodeIpamController`) that assigns pod CIDRs to nodes.\\n  - `pkg/controller/nodeipam/ipam/cidr_allocator.go`: The `CIDRAllocator` interface and `New` factory that selects the allocator type.\\n  - `pkg/controller/nodeipam/ipam/range_allocator.go`: The `rangeAllocator` (`NewCIDRRangeAllocator`) that allocates CIDR ranges to nodes, which are later used by CNI IPAM plugins.\\n- `pkg/kubelet/kubelet_network.go`: `updatePodCIDR` passes the pod CIDR from the node spec to the container runtime via `UpdatePodCIDR` → CRI `UpdateRuntimeConfig`, so the runtime can pass it to the CNI IPAM plugin.\\n\\n**CRI Interface Definitions:**\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/services.go`: Defines `PodSandboxManager` (including `RunPodSandbox`, `StopPodSandbox`) and `RuntimeService` interfaces that abstract the CNI-calling container runtime.\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1/api.pb.go`: Protobuf-generated types including `RunPodSandboxRequest`, `PodSandboxConfig`, `NamespaceOption`, `NetworkConfig`, and `PodSandboxStatus.Network` (which carries the CNI-assigned IP).\\n\\n**Network Readiness State:**\\n- `pkg/kubelet/runtime.go`: `runtimeState` tracks the network error state (`networkError`), set when the container runtime reports that the network (CNI) is not ready. `setNetworkState` and `networkErrors` are used to gate pod scheduling.\\n- `pkg/kubelet/container/runtime.go`: Defines the `NetworkReady` constant used to check CRI runtime status.\\n- `pkg/kubelet/errors.go`: Defines `ErrNetworkUnknown` and `NetworkNotReadyErrorMsg`.\\n- `pkg/kubelet/kubelet_network_linux.go`: Sets up iptables rules (`initNetworkUtil`, `syncIPTablesRules`) required for pod networking on Linux.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":3,"cache_creation_input_tokens":486,"cache_read_input_tokens":60431,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":486,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":5,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"78be9c21-f031-47eb-bdf4-f3057433a153","uuid":"c26097a9-8a60-483f-8691-dc1a872f87f0"}
